 main darshak hum yaa darshan hum! Trial on triple talaq continues in Supreme Court
 AIMPLB board kii ore se kapil sibbal ne kaha- teen talaak 1400 saal puraani pratha he or yah sweekaar kii gai he
 This matter is related to faith, which has been going on for 1400 years, so how is it un-islamic
 jaise maan lijie meri aasthaa ram main he or meraa yah maananaa he ki ram ayodhya main paidaa hue
 If faith cannot be questioned about Ram, then why on triple talaq? This whole matter is related to faith
 personal lau quran or haddees se aayaa he
 Will the court interpret the millions of words written in the Quran? Constitutional ethics and the principle of equality cannot apply to triple talaq as it is a matter of faith
 sunwaayee ke dauraan kapil sibbal ne hinduon se tulana kii
 The constitution recognizes the personal law of all religions
 hinduon main dahej ke khilaaf dahej unmoolan act lekar aae, lekin pratha ke taur par dahej liya ja saktaa he
 In this way, this practice has been preserved among Hindus, while in the case of Muslims, it is being declared unconstitutional
 court ko is maamle main dakhal nahin dena chahie nahin to sawaal uthegaa ki is maamle ko kyon suna ja rahaa he? kyon sangyaan liya gaya
 Sharia is personal law, it cannot be compared on the basis of fundamental rights
 hamen har dharm kii samskruti ko sarankshan dena chahie
 If it is bad then people should be educated about it
 mahasoos karaayaa janaa chahie ki ve galat hai or kanoon bananaa chahie
 Hindus should get protection in every Muslim majority country and in the same way Muslims should get protection in Hindu majority country
 justise courion ne kapil sibbal se kai baar poocha- pavitra quran main pehle se hi talaak kii prakriya bataai gai he to phir teen talaak kii kya jarurat? jab quran main teen talaak kaa koi zikr nahin to ye kahaan se aayaa? is par kapil sibbal ne kaha- quran main teen talaak kaa zikr nahin he, lekin kaha gaya he ki allaah ke massenger kii baat maano

 S

 "" On Pakistan, Narayanan readily conceded a differing policy vision with his boss, noting that he did not share PM Singh's ""great belief"" in talks and negotiations with Pakistan and suggested that the PM was isolated within his own government in this view

 READY TO WORK WITH US xxrep 21 - 2

 Narayanan asked specifically for U
 S
 ideas on what needed to be done and what could be achieved before the pm's visit
 Narayanan responded enthusiastically to the Ambassador's thanking him for his critical support advancing the U
 S
 -india agenda on multiple fronts
 He quipped, ""you don't know the flak i got on EUM,"" and noted that while he could often pull rank on intelligence and security issues, on other topics he did not get the same degree of cooperation from other Indian government ministries
 When asked by the Ambassador which other, like-minded Indian government officials would be key partners in advancing the U
 S
 -india agenda, Narayanan did not respond and instead noted that all matters related to nuclear and space issues, defense, and foreig policy should be directed to him

 S
 -india 123 agreement, including declaration of the two U
 S

 Narayanan responded that all pending implementation items would be completed "" well before "" PM Singh's November 24 arrival in Washington
 On announcement of the two sites, he claimed that delays were due in part to the Andhra Pradesh and Gujarat sites not being part of what the Commission on Atomic Energy had originally approved; he added that his insistence helped bring the Commission on board and that the sites could now be reported to Parliament (on recess until November), which does not have to approve the government's decision
 He NEW DELHI xxrep 4 0 1677 002 OF 003 predicted that the liability legislation would be adopted by Parliament by November, and that the GOI declaration to the IAEA would proceed in this time frame as well
 NEED MORE CT / INTEL COOPERATION, DNI VISIT, LESSONS LEARNED xxrep 45 - xxrep 13 - 4
 (C) referring frequently to his status as an "" old spook, "" Narayanan described counterterrorism and intelligence cooperation as the most "" vibrant "" areas of U
 S
 -india cooperation
 In this vein, he described an early visit to India by DNI Blair as crucial, and sought the Ambassador's assistance in persuading Blair to come to India by October ""to build on our success
 "" Narayanan noted that he had invited the DNI to visit India some three months ago, and would like our help in renewing the invitation
 The Ambassador said he would extend an invite to DNI Blair, as he was someone with expertise on maritime, joint operations, and Indian Ocean issues
 Narayanan was also receptive to the Ambassador's suggestion that he and Home Minister Chidambaram seek meetings with the Department of Homeland Security Secretary Napolitano during upcoming visits to Washington
 5
 (C) On lessons learned from the Mumbai attacks, Narayanan was receptive to the Ambassador's description of his role serving on and co-sponsoring legislation that created the 9 / 11 Commission
 Comparing the U
 S
 and Indian experiences, the Ambassador noted the critical role that the Commission played in assessing failures, correcting the stovepiped nature of U
 S
 intelligence collection, and forcing federal authorities and state and local law enforcement to work together to address the threat of terrorism
 When asked whether the GOI would be willing to share its own classified "" after action report "" on the Mumbai attacks, Narayanan demurred and noted that the report in question had been prepared by the State of Maharashtra, and that the central government would share it with us as soon as it became available
 In response to the Ambassador's suggestion that the United States and India consider holding a conference to compare lessons learned from 9 / 11 and 11 / 26, Narayanan suggested that perhaps an ""off the record"" brainstorming session would be most useful
 DIFFERENCES WITH PM ON PAKISTAN xxrep 31 - 6
 (C) In a brief aside, Narayanan readily conceded that he had differences with PM Singh on Pakistan
 He described the PM as a "" great believer "" in talks and negotiations with Islamabad, while Narayanan himself was "" not a great believer in Pakistan
 "" He added that after the Prime Minister spoke in speeches of India's ""shared destiny"" with Pakistan, he told the PM ""you have a shared destiny, we don't
 "" (comment: Narayanan made the comments above with some joviality and was totally complimentary of the PM throughout the discussion
 He made a point of commending PM Singh's intellect, economic prowess among the G-20 leaders, and self-effacing manner as an ""accidental politician"" and former civil servant like him
 End comment
 )DPRK -- NO NEWS ON DETAINED SHIP xxrep 32 - 7
 (C) Asked by the Ambassador for news of the suspect DPRK ship recently detained by Indian authorities (ref a), Narayanan claimed he had not received a report yet on the investigation, which would result in no dramatic findings so far
 He concluded that the ship had no business being there, and that the Indian government was still trying to determine why it was in the Andamans
 He noted that he could follow-up with the Ambassador with more information on the ship in their next meeting
 NEW DELHI xxrep 4 0 1677 003 OF 003COMMENT: xxrep 8 - 8
 (C) Three aspects of Narayanan's comments struck us as most noteworthy: 1) His rather blunt assertion that foreign policy is being run out of PMO, which lends credence to recent media chatter describing a marginalized ministry of external affairs under FM Krishna; 2) his admission of differences with pm's Singh's stance on negotiations with Pakistan, and his intimation that the PM is isolated within his government in involving this position; and 3) his repeated reference to seeking closer ties with U
 S
 officials, particularly DNI Blair and NSA Jones
 On the second point, although Narayanan's tough stance on Pakistan is well-known, his readiness to distance himself from his boss in an initial courtesy call would suggest that PM Singh is more isolated than we thought within his own inner circle in his effort to ""trust but verify"" and pursue talks with Pakistan, particularly in the wake of the hammering his government took from opposition for the July ""sharm al Sheikh"" statement with PM Gilani (ref b)
 This certainly confirms the risks and volatility the PM faces in opening up new dialogue with Pakistan, and means increased GOI sensitivity to perceived pressure from outsiders, particularly the USG, to re-engage with Islamabad
 On the third point above, we would welcome a visit by DNI Blair to New Delhi at the earliest opportunity
 In between such high-level visits, we would encourage more regular, informal phone calls from senior White House, State Department, and U
 S
 intelligence officials with key decisionmakers like Narayanan, to help pave the way for a productive PM visit and implementation of a robust U
 S
 -india agenda
 End comment

 Banks, which have given loans to Kingfisher, have decided to recover the outstanding debt of Rs 7,500 crore from the troubled airline
 bhartiya state bank (esbiai) ke ek ucch adhikari ne yah jaankaree di
 After a two-hour meeting with company representatives on Tuesday, SBI Deputy Managing Director (mid Corporate) Shyamal Acharya told reporters, "we have decided to start the process of recovery of loans given to Kingfisher
" haalanki, prayek bank kaa board bhavi karrwai par nirnay karegaa
 The meeting was attended by sbi-led executives of five banks and the company's CEO Sanjay Aggarwal, and UB Group Chairman and CFO (chief Finance Officer) Ravi Nedungadi, among other senior officials
 baad main nedungdi ne bataaya, ham bainkon ke samooh se aupchaarik soochna milane ke baad is bare main koi bayaan denge
 The decision comes at a time when Kingfisher Chairman Vijay Mallya has promised to give the company's employees 11 months of their outstanding salaries and also assured to resume operations with the upcoming summer schedule
 acharya ne kaha, vimaanan company ke prabandhan dwaara parichaalan dobaaraa shuru karne ke sambandh main abhi tak koi pragati nahin hui he or bainkon ko lagata he ki company ko paryaapt samay diya ja chukaa he
 The comments ullekhneey he ki sankatagrast vimaanan company par bainkon kaa 6,360 karod rupee kaa rin baaki he
 At the same time, the total outstanding on the inclusion of interest and compound interest is more than Rs 7,500 crore
 bainkon ke samooh ke aguva esbiai kaa kingfisher main 1,600 karod rupee rin laga he, vahiin pienbi kaa 800 karod rupee, idibiai bank kaa 800 karod rupee, bank of india kaa 650 karod rupee or bank of baroda kaa 550 karod rupee laga he
 The company's operations have stalled since October 1 after unrest among employees over salary payments
 company ne pichley saal may se company ko vetan nahin diya he
 Kingfisher got United Bank Rs 430 crore, Central Bank Rs 410 crore, UCO Bank Rs 320 crore, Corporation Bank Rs 310 crore, State Bank of Mysore Rs 150 crore, Indian Overseas Bank Rs 140 crore, Federal Bank 90 crores, Punjab and Sindh Bank has given a loan of 60 crores and Axis Bank has a loan of 50 crores
 company pratinidhiyon ke saath mangalvaar ko do ghante chali baithak ke baad esbiai ke up prabandh nideshak (mid corporate) shyaamal acharya ne samvaadadaataaon ko bataaya, hamane kingfisher ko die gaye rinon kii vasuuli kii prakriya shuru karne kaa nirnay kiya he
 However, the board of each bank will decide on future action
 baithak main esbiai kii aguwai main paanch bainkon ke adhikariyon or company ke siio sanjay agarwal va yubi samooh ke adhyaksh va siefo (mukhya vitt adhikari) ravi nedungdi samet anya varisht adhikariyon ne hissaa liya
 Later Nedungadi said, "we will give a statement about this after getting formal information from the group of banks
" yah nirnay aise samay main kiya gaya he, jab kingfisher ke chairman vijay maalya company ke karmchaariyon ko unki 11 maheene kii bakaayaa tankhwaah dene kaa vaada kar chuke hai or saath hi unhone aagaamee greeshmakaleen sarini ke saath parichaalan dobaaraa shuru karne kaa aashwaasan diya he
 Acharya said, "no progress has been made so far by the management of the airline regarding resuming operations and banks feel that the company has been given enough time
" tippaniyan It is noteworthy that banks have a loan of Rs 6,360 crore on the troubled airline
 vahiin byaaj or chakravriddhi byaaj ko shaamil karne par kul bakaayaa 7,500 karod rupee se adhik kaa he
 SBI, led by a group of banks, has a debt of Rs 1,600 crore in Kingfisher, while PNB has Rs 800 crore, IDBI Bank Rs 800 crore, Bank of India Rs 650 crore and Bank of Baroda Rs 550 crore
 vetan bhugtan ko lekar karmchaariyon ke bich ashaanti ke baad 1 oktober se hi company kaa parichaalan thap he
 The company has not paid the company salary since May last year
 kingfisher ko united bank ne 430 karod rupee, central bank ne 410 karod rupee, euko bank ne 320 karod rupee, corporation bank ne 310 karod rupee, state bank of mysore ne 150 karod rupee, indian oversij bank ne 140 karod rupee, fedral bank ne 90 karod rupee, punjab and sindh bank ne 60 karod rupee or exis bank ne 50 karod rupee kaa rin de rakhaa he

 Which gives the message to stay away from the temptation of all worldly things
 vahiin duusari taraf baba ke jism kaa aadhe se zyada hissaa sone ke jewaron se ladaa he
 Which is the greatest evidence of wealth gathering with both hands and being immersed in this worldly fascination
 golden baba ko prashasan se mili surakshahar saal kii tarah is baar bhi dilli ke yegolden babkepane jism par karodon kaa sona sajaae bholenath bhagwaan shankar kii puja ke liye nikal pade hai
 Along with Baba, he has a full convoy of disciples and chapats
 baba sawan ke maheene main haridwar se isi tarah jal lekar aate hai or bhagwaan shankar kii puja karte hai
 But the attraction of Golden Baba in the crowd of hundreds of Kanwari is different
 baba sone se laden hone ke baavjood beshak khud ko vairaagi sabit karne main jute hon, lekin unke is golden avatar ke dauraan sone ke jewaron kii hifaazat ke liye prashasan ne baqayada bandookdhaari pulisavaalon ko bhi duty par laga diya he
 During this entire Kanwar Yatra, these policemen also cling to Baba like a shadow
 pulisavaalon ke saath-saath 30 privet security gards se ghire baba is saal bhi apane kafile main do fortuner, do inova, do qualis, do scorpiyo, teen bade trek, paanch mini trek, ek ambulance or chaar tata chota hathi gaadiyaan lekar chal rahe hai
 Also, hundreds of devotees of Baba are also going on
 idhar, baba hai ki aashirwad dete or haath jodate puure aan-baan or shaan se kanvad yatra kar punya bator rahe hai
 Golden Babalekin, an all-rounder, is as interesting as this incarnation of Ingolden Babaka of Delhi
 baba kaa ateet or aadha vartmaan kahin usase bhi chaunkaane vaala he
 Golden Baba is an amazing all-rounder
 ek taraf vachan, pravachan, saadhugiri ke saath dharm kii dukaan chalaate hai to vahiin duusari taraf thane main bhi inkaa bahi-khaataa he
 There are about three dozen cases against Baba at present in different courts, including kidnapping, extortion, extortion, death threats
 baba ko sone kii kameez pahanane kaa bhi bahut shauk he
 However, now the same Baba, who used to sleep, used to sleep hungry for many nights
 baba purvi dilli ke puraane historishiter hanhistrishit bole to thane main kholaa gaya baba ke naam kaa wo bahi-khaataa jisamen unke tamaam chote-bade gunahon kaa puraa hisaab-kitaab darj hai
 In the name of any person, a police historyheater is prepared only when the police believe that this man cannot improve
 aise bane golden babababa purvi dilli ke gandhinagar ilaake ke rahane vaale hai
 In the same Gandhinagar where there is good work of clothes
 baba kabhi baba gandhi nagar kii isi kapadaa market main maamuli se darji hua karte the
 But people who know Baba tell that Baba's desires were very big from the beginning
 jald hi baba ne trek chanj kar liya kuch dinon tak property kaam bhi karte rahe
 But in the meantime, one day Baba disappeared and settled directly in Haridwar
 phir jab vahaan se laute to baba kaa nayaa avatar saamne aayaa
 Baba got a temple built in Gandhinagar and gradually converted it into an ashram and became a Mahant himself
 lekin mahant banane ke baavjood sone kii chamak baba ko lubhaati rahi
 Even if Baba used to donate for the ashram, he was in the form of gold
 baba ne itnaa sona batora ki is sone ne raaton-raat baba ko golden baba bana diya
 There are hundreds of devotees of Baba, like any other Baba, there is no shortage of devotees of Golden Baba
 baba kumbh ke meley main bhi pravachan baantate hai
 There are hundreds of devotees of Baba in the country and abroad
 golden baba kii vajah se hi dilli ke siem arvind kejariwal bhi kabhi musiibat main funs gaye the
 Before the assembly elections, Kejriwal's picture with Golden Baba went viral on social media
 baba ke puraane karnaamon ke chalate kejariwal apane virodhiyon ke nishane par aa gaye
 However, Baba has also taken photographs with the Chief Ministers of several states
 inamen kejariwal kii tarah hi uttarakhand ke mukhyamantri harish ravat kii tasviren bhi baba ke saath saamne aa chuki hai
 Baba distributes knowledge to the Kavadis, however Baba is not behind in sharing knowledge
 apni 24veen kanvad yatra ke dauraan baba kaanvadiyon ko kya karnaa chahie or kya nahin, ye bataane se peeche nahin hatate
 On September 29, the police raided the girls of a government school in Tonk because they were protesting against the lack of teachers in the school
 yah ghatana tonk jile ke churu gaanv ke rajkeey ucch madhyamik vidhyalay kii he
 There are more than 300 girls studying in this high school, but there are only seven teachers
 jabaki yahaan kul 22 teacheron kii jarurat he
 When about 100 students sat on the road demanding to appoint more teachers here, suddenly the police arrived there
 police ne unki baat sunne ke bajaay un par laathiyaan bhaanjani shuru kar deen
 They beat up so badly that many girls are still complaining of pain and they are not even going to school
 14 saal kii ek bacchee us manjar ko yaad karke abhi bhi sihar uthati he
 He said, "the police hit us a lot, pulled our sacks and pushed us
 bacchiyon kaa aarope he kii unhen lathicharge ke dauraan shaareerik rup se bhi pratadit kiya gaya
 a 16-year-old student said, "they twisted our chests, and abused the mother-sister
" " Surprisingly, after this incident, the police registered an FIR, that too against the teachers of the school
 rajasthan main pipuls union for civil liberties kii secretary kavita shrivastav ne sarkaar ko likhit main shikaayat darj karte hue karrwai kii maang kii he
 The comments unhone kaha, "yah maamla bilkul 'ulta chor kotwaal ko daante' jaisaa he
 First the SHO does all this and then a case is filed against the teachers and the villagers
 hamaari maang he ki vah exiaar waapas lee jaae
 " jila prashasan ne maamle main jaanch bitha di he or thana adhikari ko saspend kar diya gaya he
 Talking to reporters, Tonk District Collector Rekha Gupta said that the circumstances under which the girls were beaten will be investigated
 lekin yahaan sawaal sirf police lathicharge kaa nahin he
 Rajasthan is the state where the largest number of girls drop out before the 8th and in such an environment, how far is the atrocity on girls seeking teachers justified? yahaan or adhik shikshakon ko niyukt kiye jane kii maang ko lekar jab kareeb 100 vidhyaarthee sadak par baith gaye, to achaanak vahaan police pahunchi
 Instead of listening to them, the police started lathi-sticks on them
 unhone itani buree tarah se pitayee kii ki kai bacchiyaan ab bhi dard kii shikaayat kar rahi hai or wo skool bhi nahin ja paa rahi hai
 a 14-year-old girl remembers that scene and still shivers
 usne kaha, "police ne hamen bahut maaraa, hamaari chunniyaan khinch lee or dhakka diya
 The girls allege that they were also physically tortured during lathicharge
 16 saal kii ek chaatra ne kaha, "unhone hamaari chaati par chikoti kaati, or maa-bahan kii gaaliyaan deen
 " hairat kii baat ye he ki is ghatana ke baad police ne FIR darj kar di, wo bhi skool ke teachers ke khilaaf
 Kavita Srivastava, secretary of the People's Union for Civil Liberties in Rajasthan, has filed a complaint in writing to the government and demanded action
 tippaniyan He said, "this case is exactly like 'ulta Chor Kotwal Ko Dante'"
 pehle to SHO ye sab karata he or phir teachers or gaanv waalon ke khilaaf maamla darj kiya jaataa he
 We demand that the FIR be withdrawn
 " The district administration has set up an investigation in the case and the police officer has been suspended
 patrakaron se baat karte hue tonk ke jila colector rekha gupta ne kaha ki kin paristhitiyon main ladakiyon ko peeta gaya, uski jaanch hogi
 But the question here is not only about police lathicharge
 rajasthan aisa pradesh he jahaan sabase badi taadaad main ladkiyaan 8veen se pehle padhai chhod detii hai or aise maahaul main teachers kii maang kar rahi balikaon par atyaachaar kahaan tak jaij he? a 14-year-old girl remembers that scene and still shivers
